      % of directory writes coming from SAM
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - DSPercentWritesOther** (%)

      % of directory writes not coming from SAM/DRA/LDAP/LSA/XDS/KCC/NSPI
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - DSSearchsuboperationsPersec**

      No. of search suboperations per sec. One search operation is made up of many sub operations. A sub operation roughly corresponds to an object the search causes the DS to consider
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - DSSecurityDescriptorPropagationsEvents**

      No. of Security Descriptor Propagation Events that are queued but not yet processed
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - DSSecurityDescriptorPropagatorAverageExclusionTime**

      Average length of time the Security Descriptor propagator spends waiting for exclusive access to Data Base elements during a Security Descriptor Propagation sub-operation
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - DSSecurityDescriptorPropagatorRuntimeQueue**

      No. of objects remaining to examine while processing the current DS Security Descriptor Propagator Event
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - DSSecurityDescriptorsuboperationsPersec**

      No. of Security Descriptor Propagation suboperations per sec. One Security Descriptor Propagation operation is made up of many sub operations. A sub operation roughly corresponds to an object the propagation causes the propagator to examine
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - DSServerBindsPersec**

      No. of DC-to-DC binds per sec serviced by this DC
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - DSServerNameTranslationsPersec**

      No. of DC-to-DC name translations per sec serviced by this DC
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - DSThreadsinUse**

      No. of threads currently servicing client API calls and can be used to indicate whether additional processors could be of benefit
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - KDCASRequests**

      No. of AS requests serviced by the KDC per sec. AS requests are used by client to obtain a ticket granting ticket
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - KDCTGSRequests**

      No. of TGS requests serviced by the KDC per sec. TGS requests are used by the client to obtain a ticket to a resource
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - KerberosAuthentications**

      No. of times per sec that clients use a ticket to this DC to authenticate to this DC
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPActiveThreads**

      Current number of threads in use by the LDAP subsystem of the local direcotry service
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPBindTime**

      Time (in ms) taken for last successful LDAP bind
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPClientSessions**

      No. of connected LDAP client sessions
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPClosedConnectionsPersec**

      No. of LDAP connections that have been closed in the last second
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPNewConnectionsPersec**

      No. of new LDAP connections that have arrived in the last second
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPNewSSLConnectionsPersec**

      No. of new SSL or TLS connections that arrived in the last second
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPSearchesPersec**

      Rate at which LDAP clients perform search operations
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPSuccessfulBindsPersec**

      No. of LDAP Binds per sec
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPUDPoperationsPersec**

      No. of UDP operations the LDAP server is processing per sec
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - LDAPWritesPersec**

      Rate at which LDAP clients perform write operations
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - NTLMAuthentications**

      No. of NTLM authentications per sec serviced by this DC
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMAccountGroupEvaluationLatency**

      Mean latency of the last 100 account and universal group evaluations performed for authentication
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMDisplayInformationQueriesPersec**

      No. of queries per sec to obtain display information
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMDomainLocalGroupMembershipEvaluationsPersec**

      No. of domain local group memberships evaluations per sec at authentication time
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMEnumerationsPersec**

      No. of  net user, net group, and net local function enumerations per sec
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMGCEvaluationsPersec**

      No. of universal group membership evaluations per sec on a global catalog domain controller from non-global catalog domain controllers
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMGlobalGroupMembershipEvaluationsPersec**

      No. of domain global group membership evaluations per sec at authentication time
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMMachineCreationAttemptsPersec**

      No. of attempts per sec to create computer accounts
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMMembershipChangesPersec**

      No. of group membership changes per sec across all global, universal, and nested groups
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMNonTransitiveMembershipEvaluationsPersec**

      No. of net user and new local groups evaluations per sec when performing a non-transitive membership evaluation
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMPasswordChangesPersec**

      No. of SAM password changes per sec
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMResourceGroupEvaluationLatency**

      Mean latency of the last 100 resource group evaluations performed for authentication
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMSuccessfulComputerCreationsPersecIncludesallrequests**

      No. of successful computer accounts created per sec
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMSuccessfulUserCreationsPersec**

      No. of user accounts successfully created per sec
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMTransitiveMembershipEvaluationsPersec**

      No. of new groups encountered per sec when performing a transitive membership evaluation. Evaluations are performed at authentication time and when computer accounts or attributes are created
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMUniversalGroupMembershipEvaluationsPersec**

      No. of universal group membership evaluations per sec at authentication time
  - **Microsoft - MS Active Directory Service - SAMUserCreationAttemptsPersec**

      No. of attempts per sec to create user accounts

- **.NET CLR Remoting**
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Remoting - Channels**

      Total no. of remoting channels registered across all AppDomains since the start of the application. Channels are used to transport messages to and from remote objects
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Remoting - ContextBoundClassesLoaded**

      Current number of context-bound classes loaded. Classes that can be bound to a context are called context-bound classes; context-bound classes are marked with Context Attributes which provide usage rules for synchronization; thread affinity; transactions etc
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Remoting - ContextBoundObjectsAllocPersec**

      No. of context-bound objects allocated per sec. Instances of classes that can be bound to a context are called context-bound objects; context-bound classes are marked with Context Attributes which provide usage rules for synchronization; thread affinity; transactions etc. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Remoting - ContextProxies**

      Total no. of remoting proxy objects created in this process since the start of the process. Proxy object acts as a representative of the remote objects and ensures that all calls made on the proxy are forwarded to the correct remote object instance
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Remoting - Contexts**

      Current number of remoting contexts in the application. A context is a boundary containing a collection of objects with the same usage rules like synchronization; thread affinity; transactions etc
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Remoting - RemoteCallsPersec**

      No. of remote procedure calls invoked per sec. A remote procedure call is a call on any object outside the caller;s AppDomain. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Remoting - TotalRemoteCalls**

      Total no. of remote procedure calls invoked since the start of this application. A remote procedure call is a call on any object outside the caller;s AppDomain

- **.NET CLR Locks and threads**
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - ContentionRatePersec**

      Rate at which threads in the runtime attempt to acquire a managed lock unsuccessfully. Managed locks can be acquired in many ways; by the 'lock' statement in C# or by calling System.Monitor.Enter or by using MethodImplOptions.Synchronized custom attribute
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - CurrentQueueLength**

      Total no. of threads currently waiting to acquire some managed lock in the application. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the last observed value
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - NumberofcurrentlogicalThreads**

      No. of current .NET thread objects in the application. A .NET thread object is created either by new System.Threading.Thread or when an unmanaged thread enters the managed environment. This counters maintains the count of both running and stopped threads. This counter is not an average over time; it just displays the last observed value
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - NumberofcurrentphysicalThreads**

      No. of native OS threads created and owned by the CLR to act as underlying threads for .NET thread objects. This counters value does not include the threads used by the CLR in its internal operations; it is a subset of the threads in the OS process
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - Numberofcurrentrecognizedthreads**

      No. of threads that are currently recognized by the CLR; they have a corresponding .NET thread object associated with them. These threads are not created by the CLR; they are created outside the CLR but have since run inside the CLR at least once. Only unique threads are tracked; threads with same thread ID re-entering the CLR or recreated after thread exit are not counted twice
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - Numberoftotalrecognizedthreads**

      Total no. of threads that have been recognized by the CLR since the start of this application; these threads have a corresponding .NET thread object associated with them. These threads are not created by the CLR; they are created outside the CLR but have since run inside the CLR at least once. Only unique threads are tracked; threads with same thread ID re-entering the CLR or recreated after thread exit are not counted twice
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - QueueLengthPeak**

      Total no. of threads that waited to acquire some managed lock since the start of the application
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - QueueLengthPersec**

      No. of threads per sec waiting to acquire some lock in the application. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - rateofrecognizedthreadsPersec**

      No. of threads per sec that have been recognized by the CLR; these threads have a corresponding .NET thread object associated with them. These threads are not created by the CLR; they are created outside the CLR but have since run inside the CLR at least once. Only unique threads are tracked; threads with same thread ID re-entering the CLR or recreated after thread exit are not counted twice. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Locks and threads - TotalNumberofContentions**

      Total no. of times threads in the CLR have attempted to acquire a managed lock unsuccessfully. Managed locks can be acquired in many ways; by the 'lock' statement in C# or by calling System.Monitor.Enter or by using MethodImplOptions.Synchronized custom attribute
- **Site Status**
  - **Microsoft - Site Status - Status**

      
- **.NET CLR Security**
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Security - NumberLinkTimeChecks**

      Total no. of linktime Code Access Security (CAS) checks since the start of the application. Linktime CAS checks are performed when a caller makes a call to a callee demanding a particular permission at JIT compile time; linktime check is performed once per caller. This count is not indicative of serious performance issues; its indicative of the security system activity
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Security - PercentTimeinRTchecks** (%)

      % of elapsed time spent in performing runtime Code Access Security (CAS) checks since the last such check. CAS allows code to be trusted to varying degrees and enforces these varying levels of trust depending on code identity. This counter is updated at the end of a runtime security check; it represents the last observed value; its not an average
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Security - StackWalkDepth**

      Depth of the stack during that last runtime Code Access Security check. Runtime Code Access Security check is performed by crawling the stack. This counter is not an average; it just displays the last observed value
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Security - TotalRuntimeChecks**

      Total no. of runtime Code Access Security (CAS) checks performed since the start of the application. Runtime CAS checks are performed when a caller makes a call to a callee demanding a particular permission; the runtime check is made on every call by the caller; the check is done by examining the current thread stack of the caller. This counter used together with Stack Walk Depth is indicative of performance penalty for security checks

- **.NET CLR Loading**
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - AssemblySearchLength**

      Reserved for future use
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - BytesinLoaderHeap**

      Current size (in bytes) of the memory committed by the class loader across all AppDomains. (Committed memory is the physical memory for which space has been reserved on the disk paging file.)
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - Currentappdomains**

      Current number of AppDomains loaded in this application. AppDomains (application domains) provide a secure and versatile unit of processing that the CLR can use to provide isolation between applications running in the same process
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - CurrentAssemblies**

      Current number of Assemblies loaded across all AppDomains in this application. If the Assembly is loaded as domain-neutral from multiple AppDomains then this counter is incremented once only. Assemblies can be loaded as domain-neutral when their code can be shared by all AppDomains or they can be loaded as domain-specific when their code is private to the AppDomain
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - CurrentClassesLoaded**

      Current number of classes loaded in all Assemblies
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - PercentTimeLoading**

      Reserved for future use
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - Rateofappdomains**

      No. of AppDomains loaded per sec. AppDomains (application domains) provide a secure and versatile unit of processing that the CLR can use to provide isolation between applications running in the same process. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - Rateofappdomainsunloaded**

      No. of AppDomains unloaded per sec. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - RateofAssemblies**

      No. of Assemblies loaded across all AppDomains per sec. If the Assembly is loaded as domain-neutral from multiple AppDomains then this counter is incremented once only. Assemblies can be loaded as domain-neutral when their code can be shared by all AppDomains or they can be loaded as domain-specific when their code is private to the AppDomain. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - RateofClassesLoaded**

      No. of classes loaded per sec in all Assemblies. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - RateofLoadFailures**

      No. of classes that failed to load per sec. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval. These load failures could be due to many reasons like inadequate security or illegal format. Full details can be found in the profiling services help
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - TotalAppdomains**

      Peak number of AppDomains loaded since the start of this application. AppDomains (application domains) provide a secure and versatile unit of processing that the CLR can use to provide isolation between applications running in the same process
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - Totalappdomainsunloaded**

      Total no. of AppDomains unloaded since the start of the application. If an AppDomain is loaded and unloaded multiple times this counter would count each of those unloads as separate
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - TotalAssemblies**

      Total no. of Assemblies loaded since the start of this application. If the Assembly is loaded as domain-neutral from multiple AppDomains then this counter is incremented once only. Assemblies can be loaded as domain-neutral when their code can be shared by all AppDomains or they can be loaded as domain-specific when their code is private to the AppDomain
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - TotalClassesLoaded**

      Cumulative number of classes loaded in all Assemblies since the start of this application
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Loading - TotalNumberofLoadFailures**

      Peak number of classes that have failed to load since the start of the application. These load failures could be due to many reasons like inadequate security or illegal format. Full details can be found in the profiling services help
- **.NET CLR Exceptions**
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Exceptions - NumberofExcepsThrown**

      Total no. of exceptions thrown since the start of the application. These include both .NET exceptions and unmanaged exceptions that get converted into .NET exceptions e.g. null pointer reference exception in unmanaged code would get re-thrown in managed code as a .NET System.NullReferenceException; this counter includes both handled and unhandled exceptions. Exceptions that are re-thrown would get counted again. Exceptions should only occur in rare situations and not in the normal control flow of the program
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Exceptions - NumberofExcepsThrownPersec**

      No. of exceptions thrown per sec. These include both .NET exceptions and unmanaged exceptions that get converted into .NET exceptions e.g. null pointer reference exception in unmanaged code would get re-thrown in managed code as a .NET System.NullReferenceException; this counter includes both handled and unhandled exceptions. Exceptions should only occur in rare situations and not in the normal control flow of the program; this counter was designed as an indicator of potential performance problems due to large (more thant 100s) rate of exceptions thrown. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Exceptions - NumberofFiltersPersec**

      No. of .NET exception filters executed per sec. An exception filter evaluates whether an exception should be handled or not. This counter tracks the rate of exception filters evaluated; irrespective of whether the exception was handled or not. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Exceptions - NumberofFinallysPersec**

      No. of finally blocks executed per sec. A finally block is guaranteed to be executed regardless of how the try block was exited. Only the finally blocks that are executed for an exception are counted; finally blocks on normal code paths are not counted by this counter. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Exceptions - ThrowToCatchDepthPersec**

      No. of stack frames traversed from the frame that threw the .NET exception to the frame that handled the exception per sec. This counter resets to 0 when an exception handler is entered; so nested exceptions would show the handler to handler stack depth. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
- **.NET CLR Networking**
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Networking - BytesReceived**

      The cumulative total number of bytes received over all open socket connections since the process was started. This number includes data and any protocol information that is not defined by the TCP/IP protocol
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Networking - BytesSent**

      The cumulative total number of bytes sent over all open socket connections since the process was started. This number includes data and any protocol information that is not defined by the TCP/IP protocol
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Networking - ConnectionsEstablished**

      The cumulative total number of socket connections established for this process since the process was started
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Networking - DatagramsReceived**

      The cumulative total number of datagram packets received since the process was started
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Networking - DatagramsSent**

      The cumulative total number of datagram packets sent since the process was started
- **.NET CLR Jit**
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Jit - ILBytesJittedPersec**

      Rate at which IL bytes are jitted per sec. This counter is not an average over time; it displays the difference between the values observed in the last two samples divided by the duration of the sample interval
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Jit - NumberofILBytesJitted**

      Total IL bytes jitted since the start of the application. This counter is exactly equivalent to the 'Total # of IL Bytes Jitted' counter
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Jit - NumberofMethodsJitted**

      Total no. of methods compiled Just-In-Time (JIT) by the CLR JIT compiler since the start of the application. This counter does not include the pre-jitted methods
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Jit - PercentTimeinJit** (%)

      % of elapsed time spent in JIT compilation since the last JIT compilation phase. This counter is updated at the end of every JIT compilation phase. A JIT compilation phase is the phase when a method and its dependencies are being compiled
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Jit - StandardJitFailures**

      Peak number of methods the JIT compiler has failed to JIT since the start of the application. This failure can occur if the IL cannot be verified or if there was an internal error in the JIT compiler
  - **Microsoft - .NET CLR Jit - TotalNumberofILBytesJitted**

      Total IL bytes jitted since the start of the application. This counter is exactly equivalent to the '# of IL Bytes Jitted' counter

## WebLogic
- **ServletRuntime**
  - **WebLogic - ServletRuntime - InvocationTotalCount**

      Provides a total count of the times this servlet has been invoked
  - **WebLogic - ServletRuntime - ExecutionTimeLow** (ms)

      Provides the amt of time the single shortest invocation of the servlet has executed
  - **WebLogic - ServletRuntime - ExecutionTimeTotal** (ms)

      Provides the total amt of time all invocations of the servlet have executed
  - **WebLogic - ServletRuntime - ExecutionTimeAverage** (ms)

      Provides the average amt of time all invocations of the servlet have executed
  - **WebLogic - ServletRuntime - PoolMaxCapacity**

      Provides the maximum capacity of this servlet for single thread model servlets
  - **WebLogic - ServletRuntime - ReloadTotalCount**

      Provides a total count of the num of times this servlet has been reloaded
  - **WebLogic - ServletRuntime - ExecutionTimeHigh** (ms)

      Provides the amt of time the single longest invocation of the servlet has executed
- **ThreadPool**

      Current insertion paused state

  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - SessionPoolsTotalCount**

      No. of session pools instantiated on this JMS server
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - SessionPoolsCurrentCount**

      Current no. of session pools instantiated on this JMS server
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - MessagesPendingCount**

      Current no. of messages pending (unacknowledged or uncommitted) stored on this JMS server
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - MessagesHighCount**

      Peak no. of messages stored in the JMS server
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - MessagesThresholdTime** (ms)

      Time in the threshold condition
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - MessagesPageableCurrentCount**

      No. of messages that are currently available for paging have not yet been paged out
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - MessagesCurrentCount**

      Current no. of messages stored. This does not include the pending messages
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - MessagesReceivedCount**

      No. of messages received on this destination
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - MessagesPagedOutTotalCount**

      Total no. of messages that were written to the paging directory
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - MessagesPagedInTotalCount**

      Total no. of messages that were read from the paging directory
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - DestinationsTotalCount**

      No. of destinations instantiated
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - DestinationsHighCount**

      Peak no. of destinations
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - DestinationsCurrentCount**

      Current no. of destinations
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - BytesPendingCount** (B)

      Current no. of bytes pending (unacknowledged or uncommitted) stored
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - BytesThresholdTime** (ms)

      Time in the threshold condition
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - BytesPagedInTotalCount** (B)

      Total no. of bytes that were read from the paging directory
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - BytesPageableCurrentCount** (B)

      Total no. of bytes in all the messages that are currently available to be paged out
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - BytesCurrentCount** (B)

      Current no. of bytes stored. This number does not include the pending bytes
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - PagingAllocatedWindowBufferBytes** (B)

      AllocatedWindowBufferBytes
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - BytesHighCount** (B)

      Peak no. of bytes stored
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - BytesReceivedCount** (B)

      No. of bytes received
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - BytesPagedOutTotalCount** (B)

      Total no. of bytes that were written to the paging directory
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - PagingPhysicalWriteCount**

      Physical write count
  - **WebLogic - JMSServerRuntime - PagingAllocatedIoBufferBytes** (B)

      AllocatedIoBufferBytes

  - **WebLogic - JTARuntime - TransactionNoResourcesCommittedTotalCount**

  - **WebLogic - JTARuntime - TransactionReadOnlyOnePhaseCommittedTotalCount**

      Total num of transactions with more than 1 enlisted resource that were one-phase committed due to read-only optimization
  - **WebLogic - JTARuntime - TransactionRolledBackSystemTotalCount**

      Num of transactions that were rolled back due to an internal system error
  - **WebLogic - JTARuntime - TransactionRolledBackTotalCount**

      Num of transactions that were rolled back
  - **WebLogic - JTARuntime - TransactionTotalCount**

      Total num of transactions processed. This total includes all committed, rolled back, and heuristic transaction completions
  - **WebLogic - JTARuntime - TransactionTwoPhaseCommittedTotalCount**

      Total num of transactions with more than one enlisted resource that were two-phase committed

  - **WebLogic - JTARuntime - TransactionLLRCommittedTotalCount**

      Total num of LLR transactions that were committed
  - **WebLogic - JTARuntime - TransactionOneResourceOnePhaseCommittedTotalCount**

      Total num of transactions with only one enlisted resource that were one-phase committed

      Num of active transactions

- **JMS**
  - **WebLogic - JMS - Connections**

      
  - **WebLogic - JMS - Servers**

      
- **ThreadPoolRuntime**
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - PendingUserRequestCount**

      Num of pending user requests in the priority queue. The priority queue contains requests from internal subsystems and users. This is just the count of all user requests
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - StuckThreadCount**

      Num of stuck threads in the thread pool
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - CompletedRequestCount**

      Num of completed requests in the priority queue
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - MinThreadsConstraintsPending**

      Num of requests that should be executed now to satisfy the min threads requirement
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - SharedCapacityForWorkManagers**

      Maximum amt of requests that can be accepted in the priority queue. Note that a request with higher priority will be accepted in place of a lower priority request already in the queue even after the threshold is reached. The lower priority request is kept waiting in the queue till all high priority requests are executed. Also note that further enqueues of the low priority requests are rejected right away
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - ExecuteThreadIdleCount**

      Num of idle threads in the pool. This count does not include standby threads and stuck threads. The count indicates threads that are ready to pick up new work when it arrives
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - HoggingThreadCount**

       The threads that are being held by a request right now. These threads will either be declared as stuck after the configured timeout or will return to the pool before that. The self-tuning mechanism will backfill if necessary
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - OverloadRejectedRequestsCount**

      Num of requests rejected due to configured Shared Capacity for work managers have been reached
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - StandbyThreadCount**

      Num of threads in the standby pool. Threads that are not needed to handle the present work load are designated as standby and added to the standby pool. These threads are activated when more threads are needed
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - QueueLength**

      Num of pending requests in the priority queue. This is the total of internal system requests and user requests
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - MinThreadsConstraintsCompleted**

      Num of requests with min threads constraint picked up out of order for execution immediately since their min threads requirement was not met. This does not include the case where threads are idle during schedule
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - Suspended**

      Indicates if the RequestManager is suspended. A suspended manager will not dequeue work and dispatch threads till it is resumed
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - Throughput** (reqs/s)

      Mean num of requests completed per second
  - **WebLogic - ThreadPoolRuntime - ExecuteThreadTotalCount**

      Num of threads in the pool
- **Server Lifecyle**
  - **WebLogic - Server Lifecyle - State**

      
  - **WebLogic - Server Lifecyle - RestartCount**

      
- **Execute Queue**
  - **WebLogic - Execute Queue - ExecuteThreadCurrentIdle**

- **SNMP**
- **PersistentStoreRuntime**
  - **WebLogic - PersistentStoreRuntime - UpdateCount**

      Num of update requests issued
  - **WebLogic - PersistentStoreRuntime - CreateCount**

      Num of create requests issued
  - **WebLogic - PersistentStoreRuntime - PhysicalWriteCount**

      Num of times the store flushed its data to durable storage
  - **WebLogic - PersistentStoreRuntime - DeleteCount**

      Num of delete requests issued
  - **WebLogic - PersistentStoreRuntime - AllocatedIoBufferBytes** (B)

      Amount of off-heap (native) memory reserved for file store use. When applicable, this is a multiple of the file store configurable attribute IOBufferSize. Applies to synchronous write policies Direct-Write and Cache-Flush policies
  - **WebLogic - PersistentStoreRuntime - ObjectCount**

      Num of objects contained in the store
  - **WebLogic - PersistentStoreRuntime - ReadCount**

      Num of read requests issued by this store, including requests that occur during store initialization
  - **WebLogic - PersistentStoreRuntime - AllocatedWindowBufferBytes** (B)

      Amount of off-heap (native) memory reserved for file store window buffer use. Applies to synchronous write policies Direct-Write-With-Cache and Disabled but only when the native wlfileio library is loaded. See file store configurable attribute MaxWindowBufferSize for more information.
- **ExecuteQueueRuntime**
  - **WebLogic - ExecuteQueueRuntime - ServicedRequestTotalCount**

      Num of requests that have been processed by the queue
  - **WebLogic - ExecuteQueueRuntime - ExecuteThreadCurrentIdleCount**

      Num of idle threads assigned to the queue
  - **WebLogic - ExecuteQueueRuntime - PendingRequestCurrentCount**

      Num of waiting requests in the queue
  - **WebLogic - ExecuteQueueRuntime - PendingRequestOldestTime** (ms)

      Time since the longest waiting request was placed in the queue
  - **WebLogic - ExecuteQueueRuntime - ExecuteThreadTotalCount**

      Num of execute threads assigned to the queue
- **WebAppComponentRuntime**
  - **WebLogic - WebAppComponentRuntime - SessionsOpenedTotalCount**

      Provides a count of num of sessions opened
  - **WebLogic - WebAppComponentRuntime - OpenSessionsCurrentCount**

      Provides a count of the current total .o. of open sessions

      ID of the session that is blocking the request

      name of the last or current wait type.

      Process ID status

      The num of routine calls

      Num of global references

      Num global kills
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - LogReads**

      Num of database logical block reads
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - PhyReads**

      Num of database physical block reads
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - PhyWrites**

      Num of database physical block writes
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - JrnEntry**

      Num of database journal entries
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - LockCom**

      Num of lock commands issued
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - LockSucc**

      Num of successful lock commands
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - LockFail**

      Num of failed lock commands
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - GThrottleCur**

      Num of jobs currently counted 'in global'
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - GThrottleMax**

      The maximum num of jobs to allow 'in global'
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - GThrottleCnt**

      Num of jobs required to wait for the global throttle
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - GupLock**

      An indicator that the Write Demon has suspended global updates (1/0) (ijulock)
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - GupCnt**

      Num of users currently doing global updates (ijucnt)
  - **CacheDB - Performance Info - WdWake**

      A status indicator for the write demon, 1=Write demon running, 0=WD waiting for wakeup

  - **CacheDB - System Status - Current Users**

  - **CacheDB - Buffer Info - BuffInt**

      Num of buffers requeued in the interactive LRU queue
  - **CacheDB - Buffer Info - BuffReQCntB**

      Num of buffers requeued in the batch LRU queue
  - **CacheDB - Buffer Info - BuffWrtQSz**

      The current num of interactive buffers queued to be written
  - **CacheDB - Buffer Info - BuffOffLRUCnt**

      Num of buffers removed from the LRU queue
  - **CacheDB - Buffer Info - BuffWrtSz**

      Num of buffers in the current write cycle
  - **CacheDB - Buffer Info - BuffAvail**

      The current num of avaiable buffers (interactive)

- **Sql Area Statistics (Max values)**
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - COUNT**

      No of. cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - SHARABLE_MEM**

      Amount of shared memory used by a cursor. If multiple child cursors exist, then the sum of all shared memory used by all child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - PERSISTENT_MEM**

      Fixed amount of memory used for the lifetime of an open cursor. If multiple child cursors exist, the fixed sum of memory used for the lifetime of all the child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - RUNTIME_MEM**

      Fixed amount of memory required during execution of a cursor. If multiple child cursors exist, the fixed sum of all memory required during execution of all the child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - SORTS**

      Sum of no. of sorts that were done for all the child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - LOADED_VERSIONS**

      No. of child cursors that are present in the cache and have their context heap (KGL heap 6) loaded
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - OPEN_VERSIONS**

      No. of child cursors that are currently open under this current parent
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - USERS_OPENING**

      No. users that have any of the child cursors open
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - FETCHES**

      No. fetches associated with the SQL statement
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - EXECUTIONS**

      Total no. of executions, totalled over all the child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - PX_SERVERS_EXECUTIONS**

      Total no. of executions performed by Parallel eXecution Servers. The value is 0 when the statement has never been executed in parallel
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - USERS_EXECUTING**

      Total no. of users executing the statement over all child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - LOADS**

      No. of the object was loaded or reloaded
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - INVALIDATIONS**

      Total no. of invalidations over all the child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - PARSE_CALLS**

      Sum of all parse calls to all the child cursors under this parent
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - DISK_READS**

      Sum of no. of disk reads over all child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - DIRECT_WRITES**

      Sum of no. of direct writes over all child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - BUFFER_GETS**

      Sum of buffer gets over all child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - APPLICATION_WAIT_TIME** (us)

      Application wait time(microsecs)
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - CONCURRENCY_WAIT_TIME** (us)

      Concurrency wait time(microsecs)
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - CLUSTER_WAIT_TIME** (us)

      Cluster wait time(microsecs)
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - USER_IO_WAIT_TIME** (us)

      User I/O wait time(microsecs)
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - PLSQL_EXEC_TIME** (us)

      PL/SQL execution time(microsecs)
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - JAVA_EXEC_TIME** (us)

      Java execution time(microsecs)
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - ROWS_PROCESSED**

      Total no. of rows processed on behalf of this SQL statement
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - KEPT_VERSIONS**

      No. child cursors that have been marked to be kept using the DBMS_SHARED_POOL package
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - SERIALIZABLE_ABORTS**

      No. of the transaction fails to serialize, producing ORA-08177 errors, totalled over all the child cursors
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - CPU_TIME** (us)

      CPU time(microsecs) used for parsing, executing, and fetching
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - ELAPSED_TIME** (us)

      Elapsed time(microsecs) used for parsing, executing, and fetching
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - SHARED_FREE_MEM** (s)

      Shared user free memory
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - AVG_SHARED_FREE_MEM** (s)

      Shared user average free memory
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - SHARED_USED_MEM** (s)

      Shared user used memory
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - AVG_SHARED_USED_MEM** (s)

      Shared user average used memory
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - REQUEST_FAILURES**

      Request failures
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - LAST_FAILURES_SIZE**

      Last failure size
  - **Oracle - Sql Area Statistics (Max values) - SHARED_MEM_UTILIZATION** (%)

      shared user memory utilization

- **Dispatcher**

      Total busy percentage for the dispatcher
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_LOOP_RATE** (iterations)

      Rate iterating through its dispatching loop
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_EVENT_RATE** (events)

      Rate processing dispatcher events
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_EVENTS_PER_LOOP** (events)

      Average no. of events processed in each iteration through its dispatching loop
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_MSG_RATE** (messages)

      Rate relaying messages between clients and shared servers
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_SVR_BUF_RATE** (messages)

      Rate relaying buffers to shared servers
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_SVR_BYTE_RATE** (bytes)

      Rate relaying data to shared servers
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_SVR_BYTE_PER_BUF** (bytes)

      Average number of data types in each buffer relayed to shared servers
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_CLT_BUF_RATE** (buffer)

      Rate relaying buffers to clients
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_CLT_BYTE_RATE** (bytes)

      Rate relaying data to clients
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_CLT_BYTE_PER_BUF** (bytes)

      Average number of data bytes in each buffer relayed to clients
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_BUF_RATE** (bytes)

      Rate relaying buffers to either clients or shared servers
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_BYTE_RATE** (bytes)

      Rate relaying data to either clients or shared servers
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_BYTE_PER_BUF** (bytes)

      Average no. of data bytes in each buffer relayed to either clients or shared servers
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CURRENTLY_CONNECTED_CLIENTS_IN** (connections)

      Scheduling process with all of the number of currently connected clients too _IN
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CURRENTLY_CONNECTED_CLIENTS_OUT** (connections)

      Currently all of the scheduling process and the number of customers connected to excessive _OUT
  - **Oracle - Dispatcher - CUR_RECONNECT_RATE** (reconnections)

      In a connection pooling setup, the rate at which clients are reconnecting

      Total number of columns present in the memtable

  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - MemtableOffHeapDataSize**

      Total amount of data stored in the memtable that resides off-heap
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - MemtableOnHeapDataSize**

      Total amount of data stored in the memtable that resides on-heap
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - MemtableSwitchCount**

      Number of times flush has resulted in the memtable being switched out
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - PendingCompactions**

      Estimate of number of pending compactions for this table
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - PendingFlushes**

      Estimated number of flush tasks pending for this table
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - RangeLatency**

      Local range scan latency for this table
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - RangeTotalLatency**

      Total local range scan latency for this table
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - ReadLatency**

      Local read latency for this table
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - ReadTotalLatency**

      Total local read latency for this table
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - TotalDiskSpaceUsed**

      Total disk space used by SSTables belonging to this table, including obsolete ones waiting to be GC’d
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - ViewLockAcquireTime**

      Time taken acquiring a partition lock for materialized view updates on this table
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - ViewReadTime**

      Time taken during the local read of a materialized view update
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - WriteLatency**

      Local write latency for this table
  - **Cassandra - Keyspace - WriteTotalLatency**

      Total local write latency for this table

  - **Cassandra - Thread Pool - Completed**

      Number of tasks completed
  - **Cassandra - Thread Pool - Blocked**

      Number of tasks that are currently blocked due to queue saturation but on retry will become unblocked

      The maximum number of threads in this pool.
  - **Cassandra - Thread Pool - Pending**

      Number of queued tasks queued up on this pool
  - **Cassandra - Thread Pool - TotalBlocked**

      Number of tasks that were blocked due to queue saturation
- **Compaction**

      Throughput of completed compactions since server [re]start
- **Commit Log**

      Total number of commit log messages written since [re]start
  - **Cassandra - Commit Log - PendingTasks**

      Number of commit log messages written but yet to be fsync’d

  - **Cassandra - Commit Log - WaitingOnCommit**

      Time spent waiting on CL fsync
  - **Cassandra - Commit Log - xxx**

      Time spent waiting for a CommitLogSegment to be allocated

## HP
- **CPU**
  - **HP - CPU - user** (%)

      
  - **HP - CPU - system** (%)

      
  - **HP - CPU - idle** (%)

      
- **HP Tape Library**
- **Controller Status**
  - **HP - Controller Status - CPU** (%)

      Percentage of time that the CPU on the EVA controller is not idle. A completely idle controller shows 0%, while one that is saturated shows a value of 100%
  - **HP - Controller Status - Data** (%)

      Percent data transfer time is the same as CPU %, except that it does not include time for any internal process that is not associated with a host initiated data transfer. Thus, it does not include background tasks such as sparing, leveling, Snapclone, Snapshot, remote mirror traffic, virtual disk management, or communication with tools such as HP Command View EVAPerf
- **System Status**
  - **HP - System Status - OperationalState**

  - **HP - Disk IO - Queue**

      
  - **HP - Disk IO - Idle**

      
- **Physical Disk**
  - **HP - Physical Disk - Drive Queue Depth**

      Average number of requests, both read and write, in process from each controller
  - **HP - Physical Disk - Read** (req/s)

      Rate at which read requests are sent to the disk drive for each controller
  - **HP - Physical Disk - Read Volume** (MB/s)

      Rate at which data is read from a drive for each controller
  - **HP - Physical Disk - Read Latency** (ms)

      This, which is not in EVA3000 and EVA5000 systems, reports the average time for a physical disk to complete a read request from each controller
  - **HP - Physical Disk - Write** (req/s)

      Rate at which write requests are sent to the disk drive from each controller
  - **HP - Physical Disk - Write Volume** (MB/s)

      Rate at which data is sent to a drive from each controller
  - **HP - Physical Disk - Write Latency** (ms)

      This, which is not in EVA3000 and EVA5000 systems, reports the average time for a physical disk to complete a write request from each controller
- **Port IO**

- **HP**
- **3Par**
- **Host Port**
  - **HP - Host Port - Read** (req/s)

      Read request rate from host-initiated requests that were sent through this host port
  - **HP - Host Port - Read Volume** (MB/s)

      Read data rate from host-initiated requests that were sent through this host port
  - **HP - Host Port - Read Latency** (ms)

      The elapsed time from when the EVA receives a read request until it returns completion of that request to the host client
  - **HP - Host Port - Write** (req/s)

      Write request rate from host-initiated requests that were sent through this host port
  - **HP - Host Port - Write Volume** (MB/s)

      Write data rate from host-initiated requests that were sent through this host port
  - **HP - Host Port - Write Latency** (ms)

      The elapsed time from when the EVA receives a write request until it returns completion of that request to the host client
  - **HP - Host Port - Avg Queue Depth**

      Average number of outstanding host requests against all virtual disks accessed through this EVA host por

- **EVA_PERF**
- **Virtual Volume IO**

  - **HP - Virtual Volume IO - IO traffic** (KB/s)

      
  - **HP - Virtual Volume IO - Service time** (ms)

      
  - **HP - Virtual Volume IO - Queue**

      
- **Virtual Disk**
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Read Hit** (req/s)

      Rate at which read requests are satisfied from the EVA cache memory. Data will be in the EVA read cache because of a previous cache miss or a prefetch operation generated by a sequential read data stream
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Read Hit Volume** (MB/s)

      Rate at which data is read from the EVA cache memory because of host virtual disk read hit requests
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Read Hit Latency** (ms)

      Average time taken from when a read request is received until that request has been satisfied from the EVA cache memory
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Read Miss** (req/s)

      Rate at which host read requests could not be satisfied from the EVA cache memory and had to be read from physical disks
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Read Miss Volume** (MB/s)

      Rate of read data that was not present in the EVA cache memory and had to be read from physical disks
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Read Miss Latency** (ms)

      Average time from when a host read request is received until that request has been satisfied from the physical disks
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Write** (req/s)

      Rate of write requests to a virtual disk that were received from all hosts, transfers from an HP Continuous Access EVA source system to this system for data replication, and host data written to Snapshot or Snapclone volumes
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Write Volume** (MB/s)

      Rate at which data is written to the virtual disk by all hosts and includes transfers from an HP Continuous Access EVA source system to this system for data replication.
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Write Latency** (ms)

      The time between when a write request is received from a host and when request completion is returned
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Flush** (MB/s)

      Rate at which host write data is written to physical storage on behalf of the associated virtual disk. The aggregate of flush counters for all virtual disks on both controllers is the rate at which data is written to the physical drives and is equal to the aggregate host write data. Data replication data written to the destination volume is included in the flush statistics. Host writes to Snapshot and Snapclone volumes are included in the flush statistics, but data flow for internal Snapshot and Snapclone normalization and copy-before-write activity is not included
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Mirror** (MB/s)

      Rate at which data moves across the mirror port in servicing read and write requests to a virtual disk. Write data is always copied through the mirror port when cache mirroring is enabled for redundancy. The mirror data rate includes read data from the owning controller that must be returned to the requesting host through the proxy controller. Reported mirror traffic is always outbound from the referenced controller to the other controller.  If a write stream has been determined to be sequential access or if the virtual disk is Vraid 1 or 0, the mirror traffic for that stream includes only its write data. However, a random workload to a Vraid 5 volume requires parity to be copied as well, so the mirror data rate for that specific stream is double the host write data rate (one parity byte for every host data byte). Host writes to Snapshot and Snapclone volumes are mirrored and included in the mirror data rate statistics for the replication volumes. Snapclone normalization writes and copy-before-write activity for both Snapshot and Snapclones are done by the owning controller and do not pass through the mirror port. Mirror rates for the virtual disk on the destination system for a remote mirror pair includes initial copy and merge traffic to the replication volumes on the destination system as per normal host write operations
  - **HP - Virtual Disk - Prefetch** (MB/s)

      Rate at which data is read from physical storage into cache in anticipation of subsequent reads when a sequential read stream is detected. HP Continuous Access EVA initial copy data traffic for a replicated virtual disk is reported by the owning controller in the source volume prefetch statistics

- **Interface (Extent)**
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InErrors**

      Sum of the incoming frame aborts and FCS errors
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InFrameErrors**

      No. of input packets which were misaligned
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InQDrops**

      No. of packets dropped by the input queue of the I/O Manager ASIC
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InRunts**

      Frames received that are smaller than the runt threshold
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InGiants**

      Frames received that are larger than the giant threshold
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InDiscards**

      Frames that the incoming packet match code discarded because they were not recognized
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InHslCrcErrors**

      No. of CRC errors on the high-speed links between the ASICs while receiving packets
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InHslFifoOverFlows**

      No. of FIFO overflows on the high-speed links between the ASICs
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InL3Incompletes**

      No. of incoming packets that fail Layer 3 sanity checks of the header
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InL2ChanErrors**

      the number of incoming packets for which find a valid logical interface
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InL2MismatchTimeouts**

      The count of malformed or short packets that caused discarded frame
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InInvalidVCs**

      Number of cells that arrived for a nonexistent virtual circuit
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - InFifoErrors**

      No. of FIFO errors in the receive direction as reported by the ASIC on the PIC
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - BucketDrops**

      Drops due to traffic load exceeding transmit/receive leaky bucket configuration
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - SramErrors**

      This counter increments when a hardware error has occurred in the SRAM on the PIC
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - OutErrors**

      Sum of the outgoing frame aborts and FCS errors
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - Collisions**

      No. of output collisions detected on this interface
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - CarrierTrans**

      No. of times the interface saw the carrier signal transition
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - OutQDrops**

      . of packets dropped by the output queue of the I/O Manager ASIC
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - OutAgedErrors**

      No. of packets remained in shared packet SDRAM for so long that is automatically purged
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - OutFifoErrors**

      No. of FIFO errors in the transmit direction as reported by the ASIC on the PIC
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - OutHslFifoUnderFlows**

      No. of FIFO underflows on the high-speed links between the ASICs
  - **Juniper - Interface (Extent) - OutHslCrcErrors**

      No. of CRC errors on the high-speed links between the ASICs while transmitting packets

  - **F5 - Client SSL - MaxCompatConns**

  - **F5 - Client SSL - TotCompatConns**

  - **F5 - Client SSL - EncryptedBytesIn**

      Encrypted bytes received
  - **F5 - Client SSL - EncryptedBytesOut**

      Encrypted bytes sent
  - **F5 - Client SSL - DecryptedBytesIn**

      Descrypted bytes received
  - **F5 - Client SSL - DecryptedBytesOut**

      Descrypted bytes sent
  - **F5 - Client SSL - RecordsIn**

      Total records received
  - **F5 - Client SSL - RecordsOut**

      Total records sent
  - **F5 - Client SSL - FullyHwAcceleratedConns**

      Fully hardware-accelerated implies usage of the Cavium Nitrox or similar hardware accelerator such that all significant cryptographic operations are offloaded, including but not limited to the SSL handshake (at least the RSA/DSA/DH operations) and record processing (at least the bulk cipher plus MAC)
  - **F5 - Client SSL - PartiallyHwAcceleratedConns**

      Partially hardware-accelerated indicates that at least the RSA decryptions are offloaded
  - **F5 - Client SSL - NonHwAcceleratedConns**

      Non-accelerated connections are those for which no steady-state hardware acceleration is available (either because no hardware accelerators are available or because the necessary cryptographic operations are unsupported).  Because the extent of hardware acceleration may not be known until a connection has closed (mid-stream SSL handshakes might renegotiate an SSL session not supported by hardware acceleration), this statistic will not be updated for a  given connection until it has closed
  - **F5 - Client SSL - PrematureDisconnects**

      Connections disconnected before SSL session establishment: the total no. of connections that were prematurely closed before an SSL session was established, not including connections in pass-through mode
  - **F5 - Client SSL - MidstreamRenegotiations**

      No. of mid-stream SSL re-negotiations, not including initial SSL session establishment
  - **F5 - Client SSL - SessCacheCurEntries**

      No. of the current entries in this cache
  - **F5 - Client SSL - SessCacheHits**

      Total cache hits
  - **F5 - Client SSL - SessCacheLookups**

      Total cache lookups
  - **F5 - Client SSL - SessCacheOverflows**

      Total cache overflows
  - **F5 - Client SSL - SessCacheInvalidations**

      Total session invalidations
  - **F5 - Client SSL - PeercertValid**

      Total valid certificates
  - **F5 - Client SSL - PeercertInvalid**

      Total invalid certificates
  - **F5 - Client SSL - PeercertNone**

      Total connections without certificates
  - **F5 - Client SSL - HandshakeFailures**

      Total  handshake failures
  - **F5 - Client SSL - BadRecords**

      Total bad records
  - **F5 - Client SSL - FatalAlerts**

      Total fatal alerts
  - **F5 - Client SSL - Sslv2**

      The SSL protocol version 2
  - **F5 - Client SSL - Sslv3**

      The SSL protocol version 3
  - **F5 - Client SSL - Tlsv1**

      The SSL TLS protocol version 1
  - **F5 - Client SSL - AdhKeyxchg**

      The anonymous Diffie-Hellman
  - **F5 - Client SSL - DhDssKeyxchg**

      Deprecated! DSS certificate is obsolete in BIGIP.     The diffie-Hellman w/ DSS certificate
  - **F5 - Client SSL - DhRsaKeyxchg**

      The diffie-Hellman w/ RSA certificate
  - **F5 - Client SSL - DssKeyxchg**

      Deprecated! DSS certificate is obsolete in BIGIP.     The DSS certificate
  - **F5 - Client SSL - EdhDssKeyxchg**

      Deprecated! DSS certificate is obsolete in BIGIP.     The ephemeral Diffie-Hellman w/ DSS cert
  - **F5 - Client SSL - RsaKeyxchg**

      The RSA certificate
  - **F5 - Client SSL - NullBulk**

      No encryption
  - **F5 - Client SSL - AesBulk**

      Advances Encryption Standard (CBC)
  - **F5 - Client SSL - DesBulk**

      Digital Encryption Standard (CBC)
  - **F5 - Client SSL - IdeaBulk**

      IDEA (old SSLv2 cipher)
  - **F5 - Client SSL - Rc2Bulk**

      Rivest Cipher 2 (CBC)
  - **F5 - Client SSL - Rc4Bulk**

      Rivest Cipher 4 (CBC)
  - **F5 - Client SSL - NullDigest**

      No message authentication
  - **F5 - Client SSL - Md5Digest**

      Message Digest 5
  - **F5 - Client SSL - ShaDigest**

      Secure Hash Algorithm
  - **F5 - Client SSL - Notssl**

      Total bad client greetings
  - **F5 - Client SSL - EdhRsaKeyxchg**

      Ephemeral Diffie-Hellman w/ RSA cert
  - **F5 - Client SSL - TotConns5s**

      Average total SSL connections from client-side to the system in last five seconds
  - **F5 - Client SSL - TotConns1m**

      Average total SSL connections from client-side to the system in last one minute
  - **F5 - Client SSL - TotConns5m**

      Average total SSL connections from client-side to the system in last five minutes

- **Local Virtual server**
- **TMM rejects**
  - **F5 - TMM rejects - Name**

      
  - **F5 - TMM rejects - MaintenanceModeDeny**

      Connection requests rejected because the virtual server was in maintenance mode. 
  - **F5 - TMM rejects - MaxConnVirtualAddrDeny**

      Connection requests rejected because they exceeded connection limit for a virtual server address
  - **F5 - TMM rejects - MaxConnVirtualPathDeny**

      Connection requests rejected because they exceeded connection limit for a virtual server (IP:port)
  - **F5 - TMM rejects - VirtualServerNonSynDeny**

      Packets that are not connection requests and are destined for a virtual server that has no connection for the client address
  - **F5 - TMM rejects - NoHandlerDeny**

      Incoming packets that could not be processed by a a virtual server, NAT, or SNAT
  - **F5 - TMM rejects - LicenseDeny**

      Packets which were dropped due to exceeding licensing limitations

- **IP**
  - **F5 - IP - Tx**

      Total transmitted datagrams to interfaces
  - **F5 - IP - Rx**

      Total received datagrams from interfaces
  - **F5 - IP - Dropped**

      Total dropped datagrams
  - **F5 - IP - RxFrag**

      Received IP datagrams that have been successfully fragmented at this entity
  - **F5 - IP - RxFragDropped**

      Received IP datagrams that have been dropped     because they needed to be fragmented at this entity but could not be
  - **F5 - IP - TxFrag**

      Transmitted IP datagrams that have been successfully fragmented at this entity
  - **F5 - IP - TxFragDropped**

      Transmitted IP datagrams that have been dropped     because they needed to be fragmented at this entity but could not be
  - **F5 - IP - Reassembled**

      IP datagrams successfully reassembled
  - **F5 - IP - ErrCksum**

      Datagrams discarded due to errors in their IP headers, bad checksums
  - **F5 - IP - ErrLen**

      IP datagrams discarded due to errors in their IP headers, bad length
  - **F5 - IP - ErrMem**

      No. of memory allocation errors in the packet process
  - **F5 - IP - ErrRtx**

      No. of routing errors
  - **F5 - IP - ErrProto**

      IP datagrams discarded due to errors in their protocols
  - **F5 - IP - ErrOpt**

      Errors in options
  - **F5 - IP - ErrReassembledTooLong**

      IP datagrams discarded due to errors of reassembled too long

- **Http**
  - **F5 - Http - CookiePersistInserts**

      No. of successful attempts to insert HTTP headers for cookie persistence (set-cookie header insertions)
  - **F5 - Http - Resp2xxCnt**

      Server-side responses in range of 200 to 206 (successful responses)
  - **F5 - Http - Resp3xxCnt**

      Server-side responses in range of 300 to 307 (redirection responses)
  - **F5 - Http - Resp4xxCnt**

      Server-side responses in range of 400 to 417  (client errors)
  - **F5 - Http - Resp5xxCnt**

      Server-side responses in range of 500 to 505 (server errors)
  - **F5 - Http - NumberReqs**

      Total HTTP requests
  - **F5 - Http - GetReqs**

      Total HTTP get requests
  - **F5 - Http - PostReqs**

      Total HTTP post requests
  - **F5 - Http - V9Reqs**

      Total version 9 requests
  - **F5 - Http - V10Reqs**

      Total version 10 requests
  - **F5 - Http - V11Reqs**

      Total version 11 requests
  - **F5 - Http - V9Resp**

      Total version 9 responses
  - **F5 - Http - V10Resp**

      Total version 10 responses
  - **F5 - Http - V11Resp**

      Total version 11 responses
  - **F5 - Http - MaxKeepaliveReq**

      Max no. of requests made in a connection
  - **F5 - Http - RespBucket1k**

      No. of responses under 1k
  - **F5 - Http - RespBucket4k**

      No. of responses under 1 - 4k
  - **F5 - Http - RespBucket16k**

      No. of responses under 4 - 16k
  - **F5 - Http - RespBucket32k**

      No. of responses under 16 - 32k
  - **F5 - Http - PrecompressBytes**

      Response bytes before compression has taken place
  - **F5 - Http - PostcompressBytes**

      Response bytes after compression has taken place
  - **F5 - Http - NullCompressBytes**

      Bytes subjected to NULL compression (for license enforcement)
  - **F5 - Http - HtmlPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: HTML
  - **F5 - Http - HtmlPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: HTML
  - **F5 - Http - CssPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: CSS
  - **F5 - Http - CssPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: CSS
  - **F5 - Http - JsPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Javascript
  - **F5 - Http - JsPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Javascript
  - **F5 - Http - XmlPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: XML
  - **F5 - Http - XmlPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: XML
  - **F5 - Http - SgmlPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: SGML
  - **F5 - Http - SgmlPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: SGML
  - **F5 - Http - PlainPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Plain
  - **F5 - Http - PlainPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Plain
  - **F5 - Http - OctetPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Octet stream
  - **F5 - Http - OctetPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Octet stream
  - **F5 - Http - ImagePrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Images
  - **F5 - Http - ImagePostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Images
  - **F5 - Http - VideoPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Video files
  - **F5 - Http - VideoPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Video files
  - **F5 - Http - AudioPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Audio files
  - **F5 - Http - AudioPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: Audio files
  - **F5 - Http - OtherPrecompressBytes**

      Precompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: other than HTML, CSS, Javascript, XML, SGML, Plain, Images, Video files, Audio files
  - **F5 - Http - OtherPostcompressBytes**

      Postcompressed bytes for the MIME-Types: other than HTML, CSS, Javascript, XML, SGML, Plain, Images, Video files, Audio files
  - **F5 - Http - RamcacheHits**

      No. of RAM cache hits
  - **F5 - Http - RamcacheMisses**

      No. of RAM cache misses, excluding un-cacheable data

      Total RAM cache misses

      No. of RAM cache hits in bytes
  - **F5 - Http - RamcacheMissBytes**

      No. of RAM cache misses in bytes, excluding un-cacheable data
  - **F5 - Http - RamcacheMissBytesAll**

      Total RAM cache misses in bytes

      The Ram cache current size

      No. of items stored in Ram cache

- **Server SSL**
  - **F5 - Server SSL - CurConns**

      Current no. of concurrent connections with established SSL sessions being maintained by the filter
  - **F5 - Server SSL - MaxConns**

      Max no. of concurrent connections with established SSL sessions being maintained by the filter
  - **F5 - Server SSL - CurNativeConns**

      Current no. of concurrent native connections with established SSL sessions being maintained by the filter
  - **F5 - Server SSL - MaxNativeConns**

      Max no. of concurrent native connections with established SSL sessions being maintained by the filter
  - **F5 - Server SSL - TotNativeConns**

      Total concurrent native connections with established SSL sessions being maintained by the filter
  - **F5 - Server SSL - CurCompatConns**

      Current no. of concurrent compat connections with established SSL sessions being maintained by the filter
  - **F5 - Server SSL - MaxCompatConns**

      Max no. of concurrent compat connections with established SSL sessions being maintained by the filter
  - **F5 - Server SSL - TotCompatConns**

      Total concurrent compat connections with established SSL sessions being maintained by the filter
  - **F5 - Server SSL - EncryptedBytesIn**

      Encrypted bytes received
  - **F5 - Server SSL - EncryptedBytesOut**

      Encrypted bytes sent
  - **F5 - Server SSL - DecryptedBytesIn**

      Descrypted bytes received
  - **F5 - Server SSL - DecryptedBytesOut**

      Descrypted bytes sent
  - **F5 - Server SSL - RecordsIn**

      Total records received
  - **F5 - Server SSL - RecordsOut**

      Total records sent
  - **F5 - Server SSL - FullyHwAcceleratedConns**

      Fully hardware-accelerated implies usage of the Cavium Nitrox or similar hardware accelerator such that all significant cryptographic operations are offloaded, including but not limited to the SSL handshake (at least the RSA/DSA/DH operations) and record processing (at least the bulk cipher plus MAC)
  - **F5 - Server SSL - PartiallyHwAcceleratedConns**

      Partially hardware-accelerated indicates that at least the RSA decryptions are offloaded
  - **F5 - Server SSL - NonHwAcceleratedConns**

      Non-accelerated connections are those for which no steady-state hardware acceleration is available (either because no hardware accelerators are available or because the necessary cryptographic operations are unsupported).  Because the extent of hardware acceleration may not be known until a connection has closed (mid-stream SSL handshakes might renegotiate an SSL session not supported by hardware acceleration), this statistic will not be updated for a  given connection until it has closed
  - **F5 - Server SSL - PrematureDisconnects**

      Connections disconnected before SSL session establishment: the total no. of connections that were prematurely closed before an SSL session was established, not including connections in pass-through mode
  - **F5 - Server SSL - MidstreamRenegotiations**

      No. of mid-stream SSL re-negotiations, not including initial SSL session establishment
  - **F5 - Server SSL - SessCacheCurEntries**

      No. of the current entries in this cache
  - **F5 - Server SSL - SessCacheHits**

      Total cache hits
  - **F5 - Server SSL - SessCacheLookups**

      Total cache lookups
  - **F5 - Server SSL - SessCacheOverflows**

      Total cache overflows
  - **F5 - Server SSL - SessCacheInvalidations**

      Total session invalidations
  - **F5 - Server SSL - PeercertValid**

      Total valid certificates
  - **F5 - Server SSL - PeercertInvalid**

      Total invalid certificates
  - **F5 - Server SSL - PeercertNone**

      Total connections without certificates
  - **F5 - Server SSL - HandshakeFailures**

      Total handshake failures
  - **F5 - Server SSL - BadRecords**

      Total bad records
  - **F5 - Server SSL - FatalAlerts**

      Total fatal alerts
  - **F5 - Server SSL - AdhKeyxchg**

      The anonymous Diffie-Hellman
  - **F5 - Server SSL - DhRsaKeyxchg**

      The diffie-Hellman w/ RSA certificate
  - **F5 - Server SSL - DssKeyxchg**

      Deprecated! DSS certificate is obsolete in BIGIP.     The DSS certificate
  - **F5 - Server SSL - EdhDssKeyxchg**

      Deprecated! DSS certificate is obsolete in BIGIP.     The ephemeral Diffie-Hellman w/ DSS cert
  - **F5 - Server SSL - RsaKeyxchg**

      The RSA certificate
  - **F5 - Server SSL - NullBulk**

      No encryption
  - **F5 - Server SSL - AesBulk**

      Advances Encryption Standard (CBC)
  - **F5 - Server SSL - DesBulk**

      Digital Encryption Standard (CBC)
  - **F5 - Server SSL - IdeaBulk**

      IDEA (old SSLv2 cipher)
  - **F5 - Server SSL - Rc2Bulk**

      Rivest Cipher 2 (CBC)
  - **F5 - Server SSL - Rc4Bulk**

      Rivest Cipher 4 (CBC)
  - **F5 - Server SSL - NullDigest**

      No message authentication
  - **F5 - Server SSL - Md5Digest**

      Message Digest 5
  - **F5 - Server SSL - ShaDigest**

      Secure Hash Algorithm
  - **F5 - Server SSL - Notssl**

      Total bad client greetings
  - **F5 - Server SSL - EdhRsaKeyxchg**

      Ephemeral Diffie-Hellman w/ RSA cert

  - **Cisco - Jitter - OW-SD-Max** (ms)

  - **Cisco - Jitter - OW-DS-Max** (ms)

  - **Cisco - Jitter - SD-Positive-Max** (ms)

  - **Cisco - Jitter - SD-Negative-Max** (ms)

      Loss packets when sent from dest to source
