## Overture
- **Alarms**
  - **Overture - Alarms - Info**

      Total no. of info alarms
  - **Overture - Alarms - Minor**

      Total no. of minor alarms
  - **Overture - Alarms - Major**

      Total no. of major alarms
  - **Overture - Alarms - Critical**

      Total no. of critical alarms
  - **Overture - Alarms - Total**

      Total no. of alarms
- **CPU**
  - **Overture - CPU - Current** (%)

      Current CPU usage
  - **Overture - CPU - Avg15s** (%)

      Average CPU usage over last 15 seconds
  - **Overture - CPU - Avg30s** (%)

      Average CPU usage over last 30 seconds
  - **Overture - CPU - Avg60s** (%)

      Average CPU usage over last 60 seconds
  - **Overture - CPU - Avg900s** (%)

      Average CPU usage over last 900 seconds
- **Overture**
- **Port receive statistics**
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - BytesGood**

      No. of bytes transmitted by the port in good packets. The count includes the 4 CRC bytes but does not include the preamble or SFD bytes. A good packet is one that has been transmitted successfully (not aborted) with a good CRC. It is assumed that all transmit packets are properly sized, 64 bytes (after any padding) to maxsize bytes long
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - BytesTotal**

      No. of bytes transmitted by the port in good and bad packets. The count includes the 4 CRC bytes but does not include the preamble or SFD bytes. Bad packets include normal collisions, late collisions, and FIFO underflows. For collisions, all bytes transmitted before the start of the collision as well as the colliding and jam bytes are counted. For FIFO underflows, all bytes actually transmitted are counted
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - UnicastPkts**

      Good unicast packets transmitted by this port.  Good unicast packets are packets that are not dropped and have a good CRC. Unicast packets are identified by having a 0 in the least significant bit of the first byte of the destination address (i.e.  the first bit transmitted is a 0)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - MulticastPkts**

      Good multicast packets transmitted by this port (good means not dropped and valid CRC). Multicast packets are identified by having a 1 in the least significant bit of the first byte of the destination address (i.e. the first bit transmitted is a 1). Broadcast packets are not included in this count
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - BroadcastPkts**

      Good broadcast packets transmitted by this port (good means not dropped and valid CRC). Broadcast packets are identified by a destination address of all 1
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - PauseFrames**

      Good flow control pause packets transmitted by this port (good means not dropped and valid CRC). Flow control pause packets are identified by a type of 0x8808 and an opcode field of 0x0001
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - TaggedFrames**

      Good VLAN packets transmitted by this port (good means not dropped and valid CRC). VLAN packets are identified by a type field equal to 0x8100 in the outer VLAN tag
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - CRCErrors**

      Transmitted packets with a bad non-appended CRC field. This count doesn't include any packets with a bad CRC due to a FIFO underflow
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Deferred**

      No. of packets that were deferred on the first transmit attempt due to the medium being busy. Packets with subsequent deferrals (for instance, after a collision back off) are not counted. Whether the packet is eventually transmitted successfully or not is irrelevant to this counter. Packets dropped due to excess deferral that occur during the initial transmit attempt are not counted
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - ExcessiveDeferrals**

      No. of packets dropped by this port due to excessive deferral. The deferral time starts at the beginning of each transmission attempt and ends when the transmission starts (regardless of collisions). The deferral is excessive if more than 3036 byte times have passed without the transmission starting
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - SingleCollisions**

      No. of times a packet is successfully transmitted from this port after experiencing a single collision.  This count does not include erroneous (dropped) packets
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - MultipleCollisions**

      No. of times a packet is successfully transmitted from this port after experiencing multiple collisions.  This count does not include erroneous (dropped) packets and also does not include packets dropped due to excess collisions
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - ExcessiveCollisions**

      No. of packets dropped by this port due to excess collisions (number of collisions equals MaxRetry+1). This count does not include packets dropped due to FIFO underflow or late collisions (even if the late collision is also an excessive collision)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - LateCollisions**

      No. of packets dropped by this port due to late collisions. A late collision is a collision that occurs after the collision window time (normally 512-bit times). This count does not include packets dropped due to FIFO underflow. Late collisions are not retried
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - NormalCollisions**

      No. of normal collisions that have occurred on this port during all transmission attempts. FIFO underflows, late collisions and collisions that occur while this port is not trying to transmit are not counted. This count does not include collisions during half-duplex back pressure
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - FifoErrors**

      No. of packets dropped by this port due to an underflow in the transmit FIFO. When an underflow is detected, transmission is immediately aborted after sending a known bad (inverted) CRC sequence. The FIFO underflow error takes precedence over all other errors if this counter is incremented, then none of the other packet type counters are incremented
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts64**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were exactly 64 bytes in length (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts65to127**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 65 to 127 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts128to255**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 128 to 255 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts256to511**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 256 to 511 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts512to1023**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 512 to 1023 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts1024to1518**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 1024 to 1518 bytes in length (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts1519to2047**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 1519 to 2047 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts2048to4095**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 2048 to 4095 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts4096to8191**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 4096 to 8191 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - Pkts8192andMore**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were greater than 8192 bytes in length (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port receive statistics - PktsLarge**

      Total no. of large packets transmitted by this port. Define the size of large packets on the Port configuration
- **PAA Probe Packet Loss Results**
  - **Overture - PAA Probe Packet Loss Results - PacketLostNE** (%)

      
  - **Overture - PAA Probe Packet Loss Results - PacketLostFE** (%)

      
- **Shaper code point statistics**
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - FwdOctets** (bytes)

      No. of octets forwarded without delay
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - FwdPkts** (packets)

      No. of packets forwarded without delay
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - FwdRate** (Mbps)

      Bit rate in Mbps forwarded without delay
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - DelayedOctets** (bytes)

      No. of octets enqueued
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - DelayedPkts** (packets)

      No. of packets enqueued
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - DelayedRate** (Mbps)

      Bit rate in Mbps enqueued
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - OverflowOctets** (bytes)

      No. of octets dropped due to the queue overflow
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - OverflowPkts** (packets)

      No. of packets dropped due to the queue overflow
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - OverflowRate** (Mbps)

      Bit rate in Mbps dropped due to the queue overflow
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - QMgmtDropOctets** (bytes)

      No. of octets dropped by the queue management algorithm
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - QMgmtDropPkts** (packets)

      No. of packets dropped by the queue management algorithm
  - **Overture - Shaper code point statistics - QMgmtDropRate** (Mbps)

      Bit rate in Mbps dropped by the queue management algorithm
- **Port transmit statistics**
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - BytesGood**

      No. of bytes transmitted by the port in good packets. The count includes the 4 CRC bytes but does not include the preamble or SFD bytes. A good packet is one that has been transmitted successfully (not aborted) with a good CRC. It is assumed that all transmit packets are properly sized, 64 bytes (after any padding) to maxsize bytes long
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - BytesTotal**

      No. of bytes transmitted by the port in good and bad packets. The count includes the 4 CRC bytes but does not include the preamble or SFD bytes. Bad packets include normal collisions, late collisions, and FIFO underflows. For collisions, all bytes transmitted before the start of the collision as well as the colliding and jam bytes are counted. For FIFO underflows, all bytes actually transmitted are counted
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - UnicastPkts**

      Good unicast packets transmitted by this port.  Good unicast packets are packets that are not dropped and have a good CRC. Unicast packets are identified by having a 0 in the least significant bit of the first byte of the destination address (i.e.  the first bit transmitted is a 0)
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - MulticastPkts**

      Good multicast packets transmitted by this port (good means not dropped and valid CRC). Multicast packets are identified by having a 1 in the least significant bit of the first byte of the destination address (i.e. the first bit transmitted is a 1). Broadcast packets are not included in this count
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - BroadcastPkts**

      Good broadcast packets transmitted by this port (good means not dropped and valid CRC). Broadcast packets are identified by a destination address of all 1
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - PauseFrames**

      Good flow control pause packets transmitted by this port (good means not dropped and valid CRC). Flow control pause packets are identified by a type of 0x8808 and an opcode field of 0x0001
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - TaggedFrames**

      Good VLAN packets transmitted by this port (good means not dropped and valid CRC). VLAN packets are identified by a type field equal to 0x8100 in the outer VLAN tag
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - CRCErrors**

      Transmitted packets with a bad non-appended CRC field. This count doesn't include any packets with a bad CRC due to a FIFO underflow
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Deferred**

      No. of packets that were deferred on the first transmit attempt due to the medium being busy. Packets with subsequent deferrals (for instance, after a collision back off) are not counted. Whether the packet is eventually transmitted successfully or not is irrelevant to this counter. Packets dropped due to excess deferral that occur during the initial transmit attempt are not counted
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - ExcessiveDeferrals**

      No. of packets dropped by this port due to excessive deferral. The deferral time starts at the beginning of each transmission attempt and ends when the transmission starts (regardless of collisions). The deferral is excessive if more than 3036 byte times have passed without the transmission starting
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - SingleCollisions**

      No. of times a packet is successfully transmitted from this port after experiencing a single collision.  This count does not include erroneous (dropped) packets
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - MultipleCollisions**

      No. of times a packet is successfully transmitted from this port after experiencing multiple collisions.  This count does not include erroneous (dropped) packets and also does not include packets dropped due to excess collisions
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - ExcessiveCollisions**

      No. of packets dropped by this port due to excess collisions (number of collisions equals MaxRetry+1). This count does not include packets dropped due to FIFO underflow or late collisions (even if the late collision is also an excessive collision)
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - LateCollisions**

      No. of packets dropped by this port due to late collisions. A late collision is a collision that occurs after the collision window time (normally 512-bit times). This count does not include packets dropped due to FIFO underflow. Late collisions are not retried
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - NormalCollisions**

      No. of normal collisions that have occurred on this port during all transmission attempts. FIFO underflows, late collisions and collisions that occur while this port is not trying to transmit are not counted. This count does not include collisions during half-duplex back pressure
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - FifoErrors**

      No. of packets dropped by this port due to an underflow in the transmit FIFO. When an underflow is detected, transmission is immediately aborted after sending a known bad (inverted) CRC sequence. The FIFO underflow error takes precedence over all other errors if this counter is incremented, then none of the other packet type counters are incremented
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Pkts64**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were exactly 64 bytes in length (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Pkts65to127**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 65 to 127 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Pkts128to255**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 128 to 255 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Pkts256to511**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 256 to 511 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Pkts512to1023**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 512 to 1023 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Pkts1024to1518**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 1024 to 1518 bytes in length (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Pkts1519to2047**

      Total no. of packets, good or bad, transmitted by this port that were 1519 to 2047 bytes in length inclusive (excluding preamble and SFD but including CRC)
  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Pkts2048to4095**

  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - Pkts4096to8191**

  - **Overture - Port transmit statistics - PktsLarge**

  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - ResultID**

  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - PktLossNe** (%)

      Near-end current packet loss. The packet loss is the percent of packets transmitted but not received of the Ethernet segment
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - PktLossFe** (%)

      Far-end current packet loss. The packet loss is the percent of packets transmitted but not received of the Ethernet segment
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - PktLossFePrev** (%)

      Current number of samples exceeding the limit
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - TwoWayDelayMin** (microsecs)

      Current Two-way delay average value

  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - IgmpJoinDelay** (ms)

      No. of gaps that occured in the current period
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - PktLossNeExt** (%)

      Extended near-end current packet loss. The packet loss is the percent of packets transmitted but not received
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - PktLossFeExt** (%)

      Extended far-end current packet loss. The packet loss is the percent of packets transmitted but not received
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - PktLossNeCurrNbrLoss**

      Current period number of near-end packet lost. This should be less or equal to acdPaaResultPktLossNeCurrSamples
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - PktLossFeCurrNbrLoss**

      Current period number of far-end packet lost. This should be less or equal to acdPaaResultPktLossFeCurrSamples
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - Vlan1IdMismatch**

      No. of VLAN 1 ID mismatch detected
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - Vlan2IdMismatch**

      No. of VLAN 2 ID mismatch detected
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - Vlan1PriorityMismatch**

      No. of VLAN 1 priority mismatch detected
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - Vlan2PriorityMismatch**

      No. of VLAN 2 priority mismatch detected
  - **Overture - PAA Result Set - DscpMismatch**

      No. of DSCP mismatch detected

- **Memory**

      Memory used by the system cache
- **Interface**
  - **HP - Interface - State**

      The current state of the interface
  - **HP - Interface - Rx packets**

      The number of packets delivered by this sub-layer to a higher (sub-)layer
  - **HP - Interface - Rx errors**

      The number of inbound packets that contained errors preventing them from being deliverable to a higher-layer protocol
  - **HP - Interface - Tx packets**

      The total number of packets that higher-level protocols requested to be transmitted
  - **HP - Interface - Tx errors**

      The number of outbound packets that could not be transmitted because of errors

  - **HP - Health Summary - State**

      Health Summary
- **HP MSM Controller**
- **HP Printer Status**
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Line**

      line state of the peripheral.  When non-zero, the peripheral is off-line. When zero the peripheral is on-line
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Paper**

      state of the paper on the peripheral.  When non-zero, the peripheral has a paper problem.
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Intervention**

      intervention state of the peripheral.  When non-zero, the peripheral requires human intervention to continue working.  When zero, it requires no assistance
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - PaperOut**

      indicates the peripheral is out of paper
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - PaperJam**

      indicates the peripheral has a paper jam
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Toner**

      indicates the peripheral has a low toner condition
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Memory**

      indicates the peripheral did not have enough memory
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Busy**

      indicates the peripheral is busy processing print/plot data
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Wait**

      indicates the peripheral is waiting for print/plot data to process
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Initialize**

      indicates the peripheral is initializing or warming up
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Door**

      indicates the peripheral cover or door is open
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - Printing**

      indicates the peripheral is printing or otherwise marking or moving paper
  - **HP - HP Printer Status - PaperOutput**

      indicates that peripheral has a paper output problem such as the output storage bin being full

      Name of the sensor
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - opt-sns-2-ain-type**

      Analog Sensor 2 Type {0=NTC 1=PT1000 2=0-1VDC 3=0-10VDC 4=4-20mA 5=ON/OFF 6=0-5VDC 7=NTC HT 8=-50T90 9=10T170}
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - opt-snsr3-name**

      Name of the sensor
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - opt-sns-3-ain-type**

      Analog Sensor 3 Type {0=NTC 1=PT1000 2=0-1VDC 3=0-10VDC 4=4-20mA 5=ON/OFF 6=0-5VDC 7=NTC HT 8=-50T90 9=10T170}
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - opt-snsr4-name**

      Name of the sensor
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - opt-sns-4-ain-type**

      Analog Sensor 4 Type {0=NTC 1=PT1000 2=0-1VDC 3=0-10VDC 4=4-20mA 5=ON/OFF 6=0-5VDC 7=NTC HT 8=-50T90 9=10T170}
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - cw-fan-speed-bms**

      CW Fan speed (%) sent via BMS
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - dx-fan-speed-bms**

      DX Fan speed (%) sent via BMS
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - fan-speed-max**

      Maximum Fan speed (% of output) modulation.
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - fan-speed-min**

      Minimum Fan speed (% of output) modulation from pressure.
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - fan-pr-sp**

      Fan pressure setpoint (0.01 inches of water)
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - fan-pr-band**

      Fan pressure band (0.01 inches of water)
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - fan-af-max**

      Maximum air flow limit of setpoint from BMS or valve modulation.
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - fan-af-min**

      Minimum air flow limit of setpoint from BMS or valve modulation.
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - fan-kfactor**

      Fan K Factor
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - num-fans**

      Number of fans installed in this unit
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - ht2-hours-h**

      Heater 2 Runtime - high
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - ht2-hours-l**

      Heater 2 Runtime - low
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - ht3-hours-h**

      Heater 3 Runtime - high
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - ht3-hours-l**

      Heater 3 Runtime - low
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - engy-hours-h**

      Energy Saver Runtime - This optional point applies to energy saver units only -high
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - engy-hours-l**

      Energy Saver Runtime - This optional point applies to energy saver units only - low
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - cw-hours-h**

      Chilled Water Runtime - Applies to chilled water units only - high
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - cw-hours-l**

      Chilled Water Runtime - Applies to chilled water units only - low
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - c3-hours-h**

      Compressor 3 Runtime - Applies when unit has four stages tandem compressors - high
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - c3-hours-l**

      Compressor 3 Runtime - Applies when unit has four stages tandem compressors - low
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - c4-hours-l**

      Compressor 4 Runtime - Applies when unit has four stages tandem compressors. - high
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - c4-hours-h**

      Compressor 4 Runtime - Applies when unit has four stages tandem compressors. - low
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - cond-hours-h**

      Condenser Runtime - high
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - cond-hours-l**

      Condenser Runtime - low
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - dx-fan-speed**

      Fan speed (% of output) when compressor cooling.
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - cw-fan-speed**

      Fan speed (% of output) when cold water cooling.
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - fan-af-dx-sp**

      Fan air flow setpoint for DX unit (cfm)
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - fan-af-cw-sp**

      Fan air flow setpoint for CW unit (cfm)
  - **Carel - Integer Objects - zm-airflow-sp**

      Zone Airflow Setpoint kcfm
## SSU
- **Gps Entries**
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - Port Status**

      Represents the GPS port status
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - Phase A** (ns)

      Phase value on clock A
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - Phase B** (ns)

      Phase value on clock B
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - Gps UTC**

      Represents whether GPS module has UTC time or not
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - Module Status**

      Represents GPS module status
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - MTIE 1A**

      Represents which MTIE limit 1 threshold was exceeded on clock A
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - MTIE 2A**

      Represents which MTIE limit 2 threshold was exceeded on clock A
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - MTIE 1B**

      Represents which MTIE limit 1 threshold was exceeded on clock B
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - MTIE 2B**

      Represents which MTIE limit 2 threshold was exceeded on clock B
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - Frequency A**

      Represents the input port frequency threshold exceeded on clock A
  - **SSU - Gps Entries - Frequency B**

      Represents the input port frequency threshold exceeded on clock B
- **Gps Position Entries**
  - **SSU - Gps Position Entries - Position**

      Indicates if the GPS position is valid
  - **SSU - Gps Position Entries - Latitude**

      Antenna latitude position
  - **SSU - Gps Position Entries - Longitude**

      Antenna longitude position
  - **SSU - Gps Position Entries - Height**

      Antenna height (meter) position
  - **SSU - Gps Position Entries - Accurate**

      Antenna position accuracy
- **SSU**
- **Gps Availability**
  - **SSU - Gps Availability - Elevation** (Degrees)

      Represents the calculated elevation of the satellite
  - **SSU - Gps Availability - Azimuth** (Degrees)

      Represents the calculated azimuth of the satellite
  - **SSU - Gps Availability - Satellite Health**

      Indicates the current health of satellite
- **Output Entries**
  - **SSU - Output Entries - Status**

      Represents the output status
  - **SSU - Output Entries - Clock Select**

      Indicates which clock reference generating the output
  - **SSU - Output Entries - Clock A**

      Indicates whether clock A is active
  - **SSU - Output Entries - Clock B**

      Indicates whether clock B is active
  - **SSU - Output Entries - Clock C**

      Indicates whether clock C is active
  - **SSU - Output Entries - Clock D**

      Indicates whether clock D is active
- **Trap Object**
  - **SSU - Trap Object - Trap Counter**

      Trap counter which increments for each trap
  - **SSU - Trap Object - Trap Event**

      Autonomous or resend by user request
  - **SSU - Trap Object - Alarm Code**

      The trap alarm code
  - **SSU - Trap Object - Elevated**

      Represents if alarm elevated
- **Input Module**
  - **SSU - Input Module - Status**

      The number represents the input port status
  - **SSU - Input Module - Phase A** (nanosecs)

      The number represents the input phase value on clock A. The 1,999,999,999 is designated                                             for invalid phase value
  - **SSU - Input Module - Phase B** (nanosecs)

      The number represents the input phase value on clock B. The 1,999,999,999 is designated for                                             invalid phase value
  - **SSU - Input Module - LOS Fault**

      The number represents the input port has LOS fault
  - **SSU - Input Module - AIS Fault**

      The number represents the input port has AIS fault
  - **SSU - Input Module - OOF Fault**

      The number represents the input port has OOF fault
  - **SSU - Input Module - BPV Fault**

      The number represents the input port has BPV fault
  - **SSU - Input Module - CRC Fault**

      The number represents the input port CRC fault
  - **SSU - Input Module - MTIE1A**

      The number represents which MTIE limit 1 threshold was exceeded on clock A.  If ok, it means no error                       for MTIE limit 1 on clock A.  If not, one of the 10/ 100/ 1000/ 10000/ 100000 seconds MTIE limit 1 threshold was exceeded                       on clock A.
  - **SSU - Input Module - MTIE2A**

      The number represents which MTIE limit 2 threshold was exceeded on clock A.  If ok, it means no error                       for MTIE limit 2 on clock A.  If not, one of the 10/ 100/ 1000/ 10000/ 100000 seconds MTIE limit 1 threshold was exceeded                       on clock A.
  - **SSU - Input Module - MTIE1B**

      The number represents which MTIE limit 1 threshold was exceeded on clock B.  If ok, it means no error                       for MTIE limit 1 on clock B.  If not, one of the 10/ 100/ 1000/ 10000/ 100000 seconds MTIE limit 1 threshold was exceeded                       on clock B.
  - **SSU - Input Module - MTIE2B**

      The number represents which MTIE limit 2 threshold was exceeded on clock B.  If ok, it means no error                       for MTIE limit 2 on clock B.  If not, one of the 10/ 100/ 1000/ 10000/ 100000 seconds MTIE limit 1 threshold was exceeded                       on clock A.
  - **SSU - Input Module - FREQ A**

      The number represents the input port frequency threshold exceeded on clock A
  - **SSU - Input Module - FREQ B**

      The number represents the input port frequency threshold exceeded on clock B
  - **SSU - Input Module - LOS ERR CNT**

      The number represents the input LOS error count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - LOS CLR CNT**

      The number represents the input AIS clear count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - AIS ERR CNT**

      The number represents the input AIS error count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - AIS CLR CNT**

      The number represents the input AIS clear count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - OOF ERR CNT**

      The number represents the input OOF error count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - OOF CLR CNT**

      The number represents the input OOF clear count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - BPV ERR CNT**

      The number represents the input BPV error count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - BPV CLR CNT**

      The number represents the input BPV clear count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - CRC ERR CNT**

      The number represents the input CRC error count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - CRC CLR CNT**

      The number represents the input CRC clear count for that port
  - **SSU - Input Module - MOD Status**

      The number represents the input module status
- **Clock Status**
  - **SSU - Clock Status - Module Status**

      Represents the clock module status
  - **SSU - Clock Status - PLL Mode**

      Represents the clock software Phase Locked Loop (PLL) Mode
  - **SSU - Clock Status - Clock Tau** (sec)

      The tau is the current time constant in seconds for the clock control loop
  - **SSU - Clock Status - Quality Level**

      The PQL indicates the Stratum Level of the clock. If zero,it is invalid
  - **SSU - Clock Status - Clock UTC**

      Represents the clock has been TOD synced with GPS
- **Alarm Monitor**
  - **SSU - Alarm Monitor - Last checked**

      
- **Alarm Entries**
  - **SSU - Alarm Entries - Alarm Name**

      Text to describe this alarm field
  - **SSU - Alarm Entries - Alarm Set**

      Status of the alarm
  - **SSU - Alarm Entries - Alarm Elevated**

      Alarm elevation status

## Orion
- **Orion System Alarms**
  - **Orion - Orion System Alarms - Number of urgent alarms**

      Number of currently active urgent alarm sources
  - **Orion - Orion System Alarms - Number of non urgent alarms**

      Number of currently active non urgent alarm sources
  - **Orion - Orion System Alarms - MainsFailureAlarm**

      Mains failure alarm
  - **Orion - Orion System Alarms - Number of critical alarms**

      Number of currently active critical alarm sources
- **Rectifier Module**
  - **Orion - Rectifier Module - Slot state**

      Specifies state of slot
  - **Orion - Rectifier Module - Main status**

      Specifies status of rectifiers
  - **Orion - Rectifier Module - Configuration**

      Specifies configuration of rectifiers
  - **Orion - Rectifier Module - Iout** ( 100 mA)

      The measured rectifier output current
  - **Orion - Rectifier Module - Pout** (W)

      The measured rectifier output power
- **Orion System**
  - **Orion - Orion System - Voltage** ( 10 mV)

      The measured system voltage
  - **Orion - Orion System - Load Current** ( 100 mA)

      The measured load current
  - **Orion - Orion System - Battery Current** ( 100 mA)

      The measured battery current
  - **Orion - Orion System - Battery Temperature** ( 0.1 degree)

      The measured battery temperature
  - **Orion - Orion System - Charge State**

      Battery charge state
  - **Orion - Orion System - Current Limit**

      Battery current limit
  - **Orion - Orion System - Rectifier Current** ( 100 mA)

      Total current of all working rectifier modules
  - **Orion - Orion System - System Power** ( 1 W)

      Calculated system power
- **Orion Rectifier**
  - **Orion - Orion Rectifier - Number of recitifiers**

      The configured number of rectifiers plugged into the system
  - **Orion - Orion Rectifier - Number of failure recitifiers**

      Number of rectifiers that are not properly working
  - **Orion - Orion Rectifier - Number of okay recitifiers**

      Number of rectifiers that are properly working
